***сворачивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сворачивать.html>свора́чивать</a> (6256)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:своротить.html>свороти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svorotítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сворачивать.html>свора́чивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svoráčivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свернуть.html>сверну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to roll up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сворачивать.html>свора́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ковер.html>ковёр</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svoráčivatʹ</b> kovjór</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to roll up the carpet</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сворачивать.html>свора́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:папироса.html>папиро́су</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svoráčivatʹ</b> papirósu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to roll a cigarette</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сворачивать.html>свора́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:парус.html>паруса́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svoráčivatʹ</b> parusá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to furl sails</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to curtail, to reduce, to cut down
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сворачивать.html>свора́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:производство.html>произво́дство</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svoráčivatʹ</b> proizvódstvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to curtail production</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to wind up, to bring to a close</li>
<li>to turn, to make a turn
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сворачивать.html>свора́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:направо.html>напра́во</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:налево.html>нале́во</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svoráčivatʹ</b> naprávo (nalévo)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn to the right (left)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сворачивать.html>свора́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́ги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svoráčivatʹ</b> s dorógi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn off the road</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свертывать.html>свёртывать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">svjórtyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сворачивать.html>свора́чивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svoráčivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:своротить.html>свороти́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to displace, to remove
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:труд.html>трудо́м</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сворачивать.html>свора́чивает</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:камень.html>ка́мень</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on s trudóm <b>svoráčivajet</b> kámenʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is displacing/removing the stone with difficulty</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li>to displace, to remove

***свысока.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:свысока.html>свысока́</a> (19457)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высокий.html>высока́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vysoká</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, apparently an obsolete short-form genitive of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высокий.html>высо́кий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vysókij</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">high</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свысока.html>свысока́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svysoká</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>haughtily, with disdain
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смотреть.html>смотре́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> ... <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свысока.html>свысока́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">smotrétʹ na ... <b>svysoká</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to look down on <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+accusative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> from on high</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li>constrained (by something)</li>
<li>connected (with something)</li>
<li>halting (of speech)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chemistry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> combined</li></ol>

<li>to connect, to join

<li>to knit, to crochet
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вязать.html>вяза́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vjazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="военный термин">военн.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:военнослужащий.html>военнослу́жащий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:войско.html>во́йск</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:связь.html>свя́зи</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:связист.html>связи́ст</a></span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пехота.html>пехо́те</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> командиром-огневиком, <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:корректировка.html>корректиро́вке</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:огонь.html>огня́</a>. </span>} <span class="example-fullblock"></li>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Отважно воевали на земле танкисты, артиллеристы, стрелки, <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">связисты</span>, минометчики и представители других сухопутных военных профессий, о которых мы попытались хотя бы коротко рассказать выше. </span></li>
</ul></li>


<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="<a href = vnd.unilang:разговорный.html>разгово́рное</a>">разг.</span> то же, что связной |  военнослужащий, осуществляющий связь между командиром и его начальником или между воинскими частями, подразделениями, боевыми группами <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Рабочие отряды заняли почту и телеграф, городскую думу и казначейство. Все эти места Рощин обошел и отовсюду послал в штаб <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">связистов</span>. </span></li>
</ul></li>

</ol>

<ol><li>частичн.: телекоммуникационщик</li>
</ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:связать.html>связа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svjazátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to tie</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:связка.html>свя́зка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svjázka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:связка.html>свя́зки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:связка.html>свя́зки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:связка.html>свя́зок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>binding, tying together</li>
<li>bunch, sheaf, bundle</li>
<li>rope team (group of people moving one after the other, as in the mountains, connected together by a safety line)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ligament</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">linguistics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> copula; connective, linking verb (grammar)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">philosophy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> connective</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:связующий.html>связу́ющий</a> (25046)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Has the form of a present active participle of a nonexistent verb <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">*связова́ть</span> (compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:связывать.html>свя́зывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svjázyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:связующий.html>связу́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svjazújuščij</span>)
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:связать.html>связа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svjazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:связь.html>связь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svjazʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:связь.html>свя́зи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:связь.html>свя́зи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:связь.html>свя́зей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tie, relation, bond, contact
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:связь.html>свя́зи</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>svjázi</b> s</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in view of</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:непосредственный.html>непосре́дственная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:связь.html>связь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:между.html>ме́жду</a> че́м-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">neposrédstvennaja <b>svjazʹ</b> méždu čém-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the instant connection between something</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>link, connection, liaison</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> signal</li>
<li>communication</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:святой.html>свято́й</a> (6047)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*svętъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱwen-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">holy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:святой.html>свято́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svjatój</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)святе́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)святе́й</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:святейший.html>святе́йший</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>holy, sacred (dedicated to a religious purpose)</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:святой.html>свято́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svjatój</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:святой.html>свято́го</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:святой.html>святы́е</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:святой.html>святы́х</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:святой.html>свята́я</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:священник.html>свяще́нник</a> (4016)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">свѧщеникъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svęščenikŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> / <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">свѧщеньникъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svęščenĭnikŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сгиб.html>сгиб</a> (17274)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Nominalization of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сгибать.html>сгиба́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sgibátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bend</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сгиб.html>сгиб</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sgib</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сгиб.html>сги́ба</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сгиб.html>сги́бы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сгиб.html>сги́бов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bend, crimp, fold</li>
<li>crook <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of the arm</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сгибать.html>сгиба́ть</a> (20222)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-гиба́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-gibátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сгибать.html>сгиба́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sgibátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:согнуть.html>согну́ть</a></b>)
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сгибать.html>сгиба́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sgibátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сгибаться.html>сгиба́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sgibátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:согнуться.html>согну́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bend</li>
<li>to bend <i>(down)</i>, to bow <i>(down)</i>, to stoop <i>(down)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сгибаться.html>сгиба́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тяжесть.html>тя́жестью</a> чего́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sgibátʹsja</b> pod tjážestʹju čevó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bend/sag under the weight of smth</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to bend, to be flexible</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сгибать.html>сгиба́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sgibátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сгибающий.html>сгиба́ющий</a> (20222)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сгибающий.html>сгиба́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sgibájuščij</span>)
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ги́нуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gínutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сгинуть.html>сги́нуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sgínutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to disappear, to vanish

***сгладить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сгладить.html>сгла́дить</a> (19970)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гладить.html>гла́дить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gláditʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сгладить.html>сгла́дить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sgláditʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сглаживать.html>сгла́живать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to smooth out</li>
<li>to smooth over, to smooth away
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сгладить.html>сгла́дить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:противоречие.html>противоре́чия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sgláditʹ</b> protivoréčija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to smooth over contradictions</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сгладить.html>сгла́дить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:острый.html>о́стрые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:угол.html>углы́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sgláditʹ</b> óstryje uglý</i> ― <span class="e-translation">1) to smooth over the differences; 2) to take the edge off smth</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
